2000 scroll2 res=com.sec.android.app.camera:id/center_button_container ori=h dir=b size_down=0.5 size_up=-0.8 step=200 delay_before_up=5000
end
else
2000 scroll2 res=com.sec.android.app.camera:id/center_button_container ori=v dir=b size_down=0.5 size_up=-0.8 step=200 delay_before_up=5000
end
end

2000 scroll2 res=com.sec.android.app.camera:id/center_button_container ori=h dir=b size_down=0.5 size_up=-0.8 step=200 delay_before_up=5000
end
elseif isRotation 3

end
